I‚Äôm not sure if it was the business ‚Äòprivate dinner‚Äô events or the lack of things to do at the hotel- this hotel unfortunately didn‚Äôt surpass expectations for what a ‚Äòcrowne plaza‚Äô should be. 

As for the hotel itself, it was reasonably priced for our stay but the price should‚Äôve already included meals. That being said, if you haven‚Äôt invested, get the breakfast buffet (see picture) because the surrounding area doesn‚Äôt offer a lot of different foods and the lunch menu at the hotel is simple and short. I did get items off the lunch menu, but I was disappointed with my choice of spaghetti as it tasted and looked like it had come from a tinned can (see picture). The same ‚Äòwestern‚Äô restaurant that served breakfast also served a dinner buffet (see picture) and, although it was lacking western foods, the selection was good and I would again recommend it for your stay. However, as experienced, make sure the buffet is for guests as we were left to feel embarrassed when the buffet had been ‚Äòbooked out‚Äô by a private event with tickets, making us ‚Äònormal paying guests‚Äô wondering where to get food - the answer was a local pizzeria on Meituan. 

You‚Äôd expect 4 star service from a worldly known hotel such as this and there were certainly 2 individuals that went above the normal service to make our stay better. Bana Cheng from the reception team - Bana was like a personal assistant, answering every query and question we had on wechat about the hotel or surrounding area. James from Cafe 198 was very friendly and, as he was one of few members of staff that could speak English, he was able to give us better restaurant service and was kind enough to pack us food and snacks for our flight early the next morning as we were sadly unable to make the breakfast buffet. 

During our stay we visited the Panda research facility nearby and this was one of the reasons we chose the hotel. The hotel offers a free shuttle bus to and from the center at certain times, which was very helpful to know. 

In the daytime as it was too hot to go out, we had a spa treatment at the spa in the hotel. It was very pleasant and the ladies were helpful to translate our treatment. The room was beautiful however there was mould growing on the ceiling which wasn‚Äôt so pleasant (see picture). We also visited the outside pool and man made beach - I was surprised that the hotel was charging additional money for floaters for the children and didn‚Äôt offer beach type towels (see picture). Even though the temperature of the pool was great and it was a nice afternoon, unfortunately the sun lounges were dirty, mouldy or broken and the lifeguard was shouting at us in Chinese, probably something about wearing caps in the pool. 

The room was pleasant (see picture), we‚Äôd requested a non smoking room facing the gardens on a high floor, which the hotel kindly accommodated for. The room had a bath, which was enjoyable to use, and good aircon circulation with a massive bed. 

Although the stay was pleasant, the standard of ‚Äòthe crowne plaza‚Äô was let down by quality of furniture and decor, lack of communication with paying guests about where they can eat and the lack of tourist attractions in the nearby area. I‚Äôd recommend a stay for 1-2 nights, 3-4 is too long.

The hotel is located in a residential area, with a large lawn, a children's swimming pool, and a small church. The panda tower of the panda base can be seen not far away, and the scenery outside the window is first-class. The lobby corridor is full of panda images, which is cute. The room is very clean, and the parent-child room is full of panda elements. The children are so happy that they dance with joy. It is very close to the panda base, and the shuttle bus is very convenient. Have fun and live comfortably. The staff I came into contact with are all warm and enthusiastic. The front desk lady, the concierge brother, the cleaning aunt, and the shuttle uncle are all very polite, like a spring breeze, and feel the hospitality of Chengdu.
The hotel has been open for a long time, but the care and quality can be seen in the details. It is properly maintained and does not feel old, and the hardware is also slowly being upgraded. The only drawback is that the hair dryer is a bit old, the TV is not smart enough, and the humidity is heavy, but the flaws are not enough. I will stay here next time!

1. I was on a business trip with my children. I happened to meet my children for taking an online exam, which was quite important. I wanted to make sure the hotel signal was stable, so I found this place which is slightly out of the city.
2. Two days before check-in, Xiao Liao from the guest service center called me to inquire about my check-in requirements. I explained the purpose of the exam, and she was very cooperative in helping me find which room type had a stronger signal and which one was more suitable for our "online exam." ". And you sent me a WeChat message at about 10 o'clock the day before check-in, telling me that you could check in early and debug the networküõú. Thank you very much.
3. When I checked in, I learned that the room had been upgraded to an executive floor, presumably for the sake of a more stable network.
4. After checking in, I found that the laptop üíª could be connected to the power supply üîå for the online exam without power supply, but the power supply üîå could not be connected to the plug of another Ipad next to the invigilator. It was a bit far away and required a power *****. I called the guest service center and got a call back. To no avail, there was no external wiring board. At that time, I was really pressed for time when I ran out to buy it, and no one could be in the camera when the exam started. I had no choice but to contact Xiao Liao again, and he immediately helped me contact the wiring board and delivered it to the room, which was timely. Thank you.
4. After my child took the exam, my father, who was on a business trip for dinner, returned to the hotel and started to have a fever. The temperature was 39.9. I was "harassed" by me several times at the service center in the middle of the night. I asked for mineral water twice, each time with five bottles of water. If I have a fever, I must replenish water and then ask for a quilt. To keep warm, here is a quilt cover delivered to the room. There is a spare quilt in the cloakroom. I am wearing a mask üò∑ My father is taking care of the child. I put on the quilt myself. The service staff asked me to come in and help put the quilt on. I refused. I am a worker, no matter what type. It's so uncomfortable to have a cold. After seeing me wearing a mask, he repeatedly confirmed whether he needed help. Thank you.
5. After taking antipyretic medicine, the temperature was still 37.8, so I asked the service center again. This time I asked for ice. It was so awesome. I gave him a bag and a small bucket. After using ice under my arms, the temperature was finally under control. And by the time I checked out at 12 o'clock the next day, I didn't have a fever again. I guess I caught a cold due to the large temperature difference.
The above five points are eloquent. In a word, it is an unforgettable stay experience. I must give it a thumbs up üëç.

Before check-in, someone will confirm with you the travel time, check-in requirements, and whether you plan to go to the panda base (the shuttle bus between the hotel and the panda base will be reserved in advance for you).

2. Disadvantages
(1) It is recommended that the hotel regularly check the ceiling spray. The ceiling spray in the room we live in is probably a bit old, and the water column has many slanted lines besides the straight line...all sprayed on the face, and I really couldn‚Äôt open my eyes! But because I only stayed for two nights, I didn't bother to find customer service to change rooms.
(2) The hotel is equipped with a bathtub, but no disposable bathtub bag was found in the room, so you need to find the hotel separately to provide it. It is recommended to put a warm reminder "the hotel is equipped with disposable bathtub bags, if you need them, please ask the front desk for them".

3. Advantages
(1) When Xiaoxia contacted me about the check-in requirements and time, I was more concerned about whether there was a ceiling spray in the bathroom, and someone made a special trip to help me confirm and reply. Before I went to the Panda Base, I was not sure about the return time, and she suggested that I book a shuttle bus for me in case of emergency. Later, because I had to rush back to check out at the Panda Base, I contacted her to see if I could change the appoin**ent time of the shuttle bus. She also used the authority to help me delay the check-out so that I didn't have to go back in a hurry. It must be praised here! !
(2) It takes more than 100 taxis from Shuangliu Airport at night, because it is considered a suburb, so you can clearly feel the surrounding greenery. There are also many panda dolls of different sizes arranged in the lobby of the hotel. The room area of the hotel is relatively large, with separate toilet, shower room, and bathtub. The shower room is divided into top spray and hand-held. From the room, you can see new couples taking wedding photos on the lawn downstairs. The scenery is very beautiful. The lady at the front desk gave us a lovely gift when we checked out.
(3) On the day of departure to the Panda Base, we will confirm with you again about 30 minutes before the scheduled shuttle bus departure whether to take the shuttle bus. If you take the shuttle bus, you will be reminded to wait in the lobby in advance. The shuttle bus departs on time, so don‚Äôt be late.
(4) The lady at the front desk gave us 2 souvenirs when we checked out!
Overall, the stay is very comfortable, and I will come again next time!

I recently stayed at the Crowne Plaza Chengdu Panda Garden Hotel, which is located near the Panda Garden. It was incredibly convenient for me to visit the Panda Garden since the hotel is located very close by. The staff were friendly and always willing to help me with directions and transportation.
The room itself was spacious and clean, with all the amenities I needed for a comfortable stay. The bed was comfortable, and I slept well each night. The hotel also had a great selection of restaurants and bars, so I was able to enjoy delicious food and drink after a long day of exploring.
Overall, I highly recommend the hotel for anyone visiting the Panda Garden. It's a great value for the price and provides a comfortable, convenient, and enjoyable stay.
